country_event = {
	id = 71601
	title = "Dynamic Loc Country Bounce Event"
	picture = "crisis"
	allow_multiple_instances = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 0 } }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 0.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 1.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 2 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 1.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 2.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 3 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 2.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 3.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 4 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 3.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 4.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 5 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 4.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 5.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 6 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 5.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 6.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 7 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 6.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 7.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 8 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 7.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 8.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 9 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 8.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 9.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 10 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 9.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 10.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 11 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 10.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 11.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 12 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 11.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 12.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 13 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 12.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 13.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 14 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 13.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 14.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 15 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 14.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 15.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 16 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 15.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 16.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 17 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 16.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 17.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 18 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 17.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 18.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 19 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 18.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 19.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 20 } }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 19.99 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 20.99 } }
			}
			UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 21 } }
		}
		country_event = 71602
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ""
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 71602
	title = "Dynamic Loc Country Effect Event"
	picture = "crisis"
	allow_multiple_instances = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 20.99 } }
				check_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 19.99 }
				UTI = { check_variable = { which = itterator value = 19.99 } }
				NOT = { UTI = { check_variable = { which = itterator value = 20.99 } } }
			}
			set_country_flag = rename_loc_country
			set_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 0 }
